/// </summary>\n    internal interface ISymbolResolutionStrategy\n    {\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Performs a lookup within a single binder scope using this strategy.\n        ///    /// </summary>\n        bool ShouldContinueSearch(LookupResult result);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Captures the result of a unified symbol resolution, including resolved symbols\n    /// and any associated diagnostics.\n    /// </summary>\n    internal sealed class SymbolResolutionResult\n    {\n        /// <summary>\n        /// The symbols found during resolution.\n        /// </summary>\n        public ImmutableArray<Symbol> Symbols { get; }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// The diagnostic, if any, produced during resolution.\n        /// </summary>\n        public DiagnosticInfo Diagnostic { get; }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Whether the resolution found at least one viable symbol.\n        /// </summary>\n        public bool IsViable { get; }\n\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Whether the resolution found no symbols.\n        /// </summary>\n        public bool IsEmpty => Symbols.IsDefaultOrEmpty;\n\n        public SymbolResolutionResult(ImmutableArray<Symbol> symbols, DiagnosticInfo diagnostic, bool isViable)\n        {\n            Symbols = symbols;\n            Diagnostic = diagnostic;\n            IsViable = isViable;\n        }\n\n        internal static readonly SymbolResolutionResult Empty =\n            new SymbolResolutionResult(ImmutableArray<Symbol>.Empty, diagnostic: null, isViable: false);\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Strategy for looking up type symbols (named types and type parameters).\n    /// </summary>\n    internal sealed class TypeResolutionStrategy : ISymbolResolutionStrategy\n    {\n        public static readonly TypeResolutionStrategy Instance = new TypeResolutionStrategy();\n\n        private TypeResolutionStrategy() { }\n\n        public void LookupSymbols(\n            LookupResult result,\n            Binder binder,\n            string name,\n            int arity,\n            LookupOptions options,\n            bool diagnose,\n            ref CompoundUseSiteInfo<AssemblySymbol> useSiteInfo)\n        {\n            var typeOptions = options | LookupOptions.NamespacesOrTypesOnly;\n            binder.LookupSymbolsInSingleBinder(result, name, arity, basesBeingResolved: null, typeOptions, binder, diagnose, ref useSiteInfo);\n        }\n\n        public bool ShouldContinueSearch(LookupResult result)\n            => qualifier)\n        {\n            _qualifier = qualifier;\n        }\n\n        public void LookupSymbols(\n            LookupResult result,\n            Binder binder,\n            string name,\n            int arity,\n            LookupOptions options,\n            bool diagnose,\n            ref CompoundUseSiteInfo<AssemblySymbol> useSiteInfo)\n        {\n            var memberOptions = options & ~LookupOptions.NamespacesOrTypesOnly;\n            binder.LookupMembersInternal(result, _qualifier, name, arity, basesBeingResolved: null, memberOptions, binder, diagnose, ref useSiteInfo);\n        }\n\n        public bool ShouldContinueSearch(LookupResult result)\n            => !result.IsMultiViable;\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Strategy for looking up namespace symbols only.\n    /// NamespaceResolutionStrategy();\n\n        private NamespaceResolutionStrategy() { }\n\n        public void LookupSymbols(\n            LookupResult result,\n            Binder binder,\n binder, diagnose, ref useSiteInfo);\n        }\n\n        public bool ShouldContinueSearch(LookupResult result)\n            => !result.IsMultiViable;\n    }\n\n    /// <summary>\n    /// Provides a unified entry point for symbol resolution that consolidates common lookup\n    /// patterns across different binding contexts. Resolution walks the binder scope chain\n    /// using the provided <see cref=\"ISymbolResolutionStrategy\"/> to control lookup behavior\n    /// at each scope and to decide when to stop searching.\n    /// </summary>\n    internal sealed class UnifiedSymbolResolver\n    {\n        /// <summary>\n        /// Resolves symbols by walking the binder scope chain starting at <paramref name=\"binder\"/>,\n        /// using the given <paramref name=\"strategy\"/> to perform the lookup at each scope.\n        /// </summary>\n        /// <param name=\"binder\">The starting binder (innermost scope).</param>\n        /// <param name=\"name\">The symbol name to look up.</param>\n        /// <param name=\"arity\">The arity (number of type parameters). Pass 0 for non-generic.</param>\n        /// <param name=\"strategy\">The resolution strategy that controls lookup per scope.</param>\n        /// <param name=\"options\">Additional lookup options.</param>\n        /// <returns>A <see cref=\"SymbolResolutionResult\"/> capturing the found symbols and diagnostics.</returns>\n        public SymbolResolutionResult Resolve(\n            Binder binder,\n            string name,\n            int arity,\n            ISymbolResolutionStrategy strategy,\n            LookupOptions options = LookupOptions.Default)\n        {\n            if (binder is null) return SymbolResolutionResult.Empty;\n            if (name is null) return SymbolResolutionResult.Empty;\n\n            var useSiteInfo = CompoundUseSiteInfo<AssemblySymbol>.DiscardedDependencies;\n\n            // First pass: lookup without diagnostics\n            var result = LookupResult.GetInstance();\n            try\n            {\n                WalkScopeChain(result, binder, name, arity, strategy, options, diagnose: false, ref useSiteInfo);\n\n                if (!result.IsMultiViable && !result.IsClear)\n                {\n                    // Second pass: retry with diagnostics to get richer error info\n                    result.Clear();\n                    useSiteInfo = CompoundUseSiteInfo<AssemblySymbol>.DiscardedDependencies;\n                    WalkScopeChain(result, binder, name, arity, strategy, options, diagnose: true, ref useSiteInfo);\n                }\n\n                return BuildResult(result);\n            }\n            finally\n            {\n                result.Free();\n            }\n        }\n\n        private static void WalkScopeChain(\n            LookupResult result,\n            Binder startingBinder,\n            string name,\n            int arity,\n            ISymbolResolutionStrategy strategy,\n            LookupOptions options,\n            bool diagnose,\n            ref CompoundUseSiteInfo<AssemblySymbol> useSiteInfo)\n        {\n            for (var scope = startingBinder; scope != null && strategy.ShouldContinueSearch(result); scope = scope.Next)\n            {\n                strategy.LookupSymbols(result, scope, name, arity, options, diagnose, ref useSiteInfo);\n            }\n        }\n\n        private static SymbolResolutionResult BuildResult(LookupResult result)\n        {\n            var symbols = result.Symbols.ToImmutableArray();\n            var diagnostic = result.Error;\n            var isViable = result.IsMultiViable;\n            return new SymbolResolutionResult(symbols, diagnostic, isViable);\n        }\n
